 The incident is on July 29
 tikaaram ne bacchee ko uske ghar se agava kar liya

 iske baad bacchee ke gaayab hone kii suchnapuliceko di gai

 finland kii company echemadi global ne haal hi main bharat main Nokia 7 Plus launch kiya he
 Nokia's mobile phones were quite popular around the world, including India
 lekin ab sirf nokia ke smartphone isliye nahin kamaal kar paaenge, kyonki ek samay main wo popular the
 For this, the company will have to prove itself again, and this is the reason that new smartphones of Nokia are constantly coming in the market
 inamen se ek Nokia 7 Plus he or hamane iskaa rivyuu kiya he
 Have tried to know, does this smartphone meet the company's claim
 is rivyuu main aap padhengedizin / bild quality – Nokia 7 Plus dizin or bild quality main kahaan thahartaa he
 Display and performance - Does the best hardware make it powerful in real life? User Experience - Do you get the feel of Nokia mobile by using it? Is it a good experience to use it? Camera and battery - this photography will show what amazing performance this smartphone will show, along with how long the battery can support you, you will also know in this review
 phul rivudizin or bild quality –ise hold karte hi aapako premium divaais kaa anubhav hoga, saath hi dekhte hi aap yah samaj jaaenge ki yah smartphone durable he
 This is because the company has used 6000 series aluminum blocks in it which is known to be durable
 hamane blike copper verient kaa rivyuu kiya he
 The design of Nokia 7 Plus is excellent, its edge is given copper and it looks great with black
 camera or fingerprint scinar main copper finnish he jisase yah or bhi behatar lagata he
 Nokia's branding is at the back
 rier main vertical dual camera seoup he or iske neeche fingerprint scinar diya gaya he
 Dual LED flash is provided next to the camera
 phone ke neeche Android One kii branding he
 The volume rocker and lock keys are on the right side while on the left side you get the SIM, memory card tray
 neeche kii taraf spikar gril ke saath USB Type c jaik he or upar kii taraf headphone jaik diya gaya he
 Display Nokia 7 Plus has a 6-inch Full HD Plus display and the aspect ratio is 18: 9
 disple rejolushan (2160X1440) he or IPS alsidi panel kaa yuj kiya gaya he or upar gorilla glass 3 diya gaya he
 The display looks bright at first sight and does not bother your eyes with use
 vuing angel bhi acha he kisi bhi corner se disple dekhne main koi pareshaani nahin hoti
 The display is large and it is a good experience to watch videos and the performance of the display is also good in gaming
 lekin suraj kii raushnee main disple ke contant dekhne main aapako thodi pareshaani ho sakati he
 There are also some features like double tap wakeup that make you easy in display usage
 parformansis smartphone main qolkom snapadragon 660 procesar ke saath 4GB ram diya gaya he
 Internal memory is 64GB which can be increased to 256GB via micro SD card
 procesar ko lekar yahaan aapaki alag raay ho sakati he, kyonki is range main philhal Snapdragon 835 procesar vaale smartphone bhi mil rahe hai
 But the company has customized it in a better way, which gives better user experience
 haalanki Snapdragon 835 diya gaya hota to nishchit taur par zyada behatar hota
 Bahral, we have used it continuously and on this basis we can say that this smartphone does not lag
 zyada der tak gaming karne se yah phone garm hota he
 Although many apps are running in the background during gaming, there is no hang, nor is there any problem in gaming
 lagaataar video dekhte rahen to bhi yah smartphone garm hota he
 Switching apps means moving from app to app, loading time is short and you don't know
 lekin agar aap power yujar hai or ek saath kai heavi eps yuj kar rahe hai to aapke liye dikkat ho sakati he
 Android One improves the user experience of this smartphone
 isamen blottware na ke baraabar hai or pyor android he
 Security patches continue to be received and the company has customized it well with Android One
 agar yahaan aap kai or launture yaa custom skin yuj karnaa chahen to dikkat ho sakati he or phone hang hone kii samasya aa sakati he
 Overall performance can be better than average
 camerice smartphone main dual rier camera seoup diya gaya he
 There is a lens of 12 megapixels, which has an aperture f / 1
 7 he
 The second lens is 13 megapixels and is a telephoto
 nokia ke in smartfones kii khaasiyat bothi feechar bhi he jo contant creatre or patrakaron ke liye kaaphi behatar he
 The camera works with Nokia 7 Plus's rear and front camera, which means that you can use the front and rear cameras at once
 yah tab kaaphi mahatvapurn feechar ban jaataa he jab aapako kisi kaa intervyuu record karnaa he or aapke paas koi camera person nahin he
 We have used it, it is great
 duusari companiyon ko bhi ab aisa feechar dena chahie
 The camera does not have optical image stabilization (OIS) and we lack it during photography
 photography ke liye hamen yah smartphone everej laga, kyonki delite main to isse acchhee tasviren clic kar sakate hai, lekin kam raushnee or indoor main clic kii gai tasviren aapako niraash kar sakati hai
 Background blur is not the way it should be, most of the times and it feels weird
 company ne isamen ZEISS optics diya he jisase hamen kaaphi ummiden thim
 The selfie camera is 16 megapixels and selfie can click best
 tasviir kii quality bhi acchhee he
 2X zoomed clicked photos are also good, there is no problem
 overol camera parformens acha he, lekin ise or behatar kiya ja saktaa tha
 This smartphone is definitely the best in terms of battery battery
 is smartphone main company ne 3,800mah kii bydaree lagaai he
 Once full charged, you can run it comfortably throughout the day
 is dauraan aap internet on rakhkar web browjing, soshal media, mujeec or colling kar sakate hai jo aam taur par ek aam smartphone yujar karata he
 Due to fast charging support, it charges quickly and its standby timing also does not disappoint
 bina yuj kiye aap smartphone chhod den to, kuch dinon tak yah chaalu rahegaa
 Overall battery performance is excellent and if you are thinking of buying a good smartphone with good battery then this is obviously for you

 The German Research Foundation Deutsche Forschungsgemenscheft (DFG) was originally founded in 1920 but was re-established in 1951 after World War II
 iske baad se DFG lagaataar badhata chalaa gaya
 Today its annual budget 2
 9 arab euro ke lagbhag he
 It is Germany's most important institute for research in the field of science, as well as one of the world's largest independent institutions for funding research
 iskaa makasad jigyaasa par aadhaarit fundamental research ke liye madad dena he, jo nai kadiyon ko jod saktaa he, ekadam nae tarah ke kshetron ke daravaaje khol saktaa he yaa phir nai khoj ke liye jameen bhi taiyaar kar saktaa he
 For this it also provides large research facilities such as research vessels and data systems
 dienji kaa ek or ahm kaam acadmic or scientific vishyon par rajnatik salaah dena he
 Internationally, DFG also represents a community of researchers from Germany
 aise antarrashtriya research program jinamein antarrashtriya mahatv ke sawaalon par dhyaan dene ke liye deshon ke bich sahyog kii jarurat hoti he, unamem DFG kii mahatvapurn bhoomika he
 DFG is the head of the consortium of the German House for Research and Innovation (DWIH, New Delhi) in India
 is consorcium kii sthapana duniyabar ke deshon ke saath academic sahyog ko badhaane kii german sarkaar kii pahal par kii gai thi
 The dfg's funding portfolio and its work as a proponent of academic and scientific freedom has earned it a national and international recognition for the science and humanities community
 bhartiya-german research sahyog badhaane ke liye DFG ne pichley kuch varshon main kis tarah ke kadam uthaae hai?dfg research ke liye paisa dene vaala germany kaa sabase bada swatantra santhaan he
 Its main job is to provide financial support to universities, research projects of research institutes and all the ongoing research related work in the field of science or humanities
 acadmic sahyog rashtriya simaaon main bandhakar nahin rah saktaa isliye DFG ne apane offis kai deshon main khol rakhe hai
 DFG opened its office in New Delhi in 2006 and today it serves as a major center of shared academic activities between DFG and its Indian partners
 beete varshon main saajhedaari main kai kaam kiye gaye hai

 nae projects ko shuru karne ke liye ab donon desh niyamit taur par dhan uplabdh karavaate hai
